  <raw>VW buys one-fifth stake in Suzuki



Germany's Volkswagen AG will buy a one-fifth stake in Suzuki Motor Corp for $2.5-billion US, tapping the Japanese firm's expertise in small cars and dominance in India as VW seeks to become the No. 1 automaker.

The move is the second coup this week for ambitious VW Chairman Ferdinand Piech, coming on the heels of the German carmaker's 3.9-billion euro ($5.8-billion US) purchase of a 49-per-cent stake in Porsche AG.
VW chief executive Martin Winterkorn was hopeful the Suzuki alliance would help catapult the Wolfsburgbased carmaker past industry leader Toyota Motor Corp ahead of plan.
"If that succeeds faster (than 2018), we're happy," Winterkorn said as he sat next to Suzuki's nearly 80-year-old CEO Osamu Suzuki at a Tokyo press conference.
Suzuki said he did not intend the company to come under VW's control.
"I don't want you to misunderstand: Suzuki is not becoming a 12th brand for Volkswagen. I don't want other folks telling me how to do things."</raw>
